1货币时间价值L01
Bruce deposits 100 into a bank account. His account is credited interest at an annual nominal rate of interest of 4% convertible semiannually. At the same time, Peter deposits 100 into a separate account. Peter's account is credited interest at an annual force of interest of \(\delta\). After 7.25 years, the value of each account is the same. Calculate \(\delta\).
(A) 0.0388(B) 0.0392(C) 0.0396(D) 0.0404(E) 0.0414
名义利率对力度
答案 C
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 名义利率等价利息力\(\big(1+\tfrac{i^{(2)}}{2}\big)^2=e^{\delta}\)L01
② 代入求累积因子\(e^{\delta}=1.02^2=1.0404\)L01
③ 取对数得利息力\(\delta=\ln 1.0404=0.0396\)代数/微积分
2年金L03
Kathryn deposits 100 into an account at the beginning of each 4-year period for 40 years. The account credits interest at an annual effective interest rate of \(i\). The accumulated amount in the account at the end of 40 years is \(X\), which is 5 times the accumulated amount in the account at the end of 20 years. Calculate \(X\).
(A) 4695(B) 5070(C) 5445(D) 5820(E) 6195
四年期存款累积
答案 E
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 写20年累积值\(100\frac{(1+i)^4-(1+i)^{24}}{1-(1+i)^4}\)L03
② 比值为5设x代换\(5=\frac{x-x^{11}}{x-x^{6}},\;x=(1+i)^4\)L02
③ 因式分解取正根\((x^5-1)(x^5-4)=0\Rightarrow x^5=4\)代数/微积分
④ 回代求40年累积\(X=100\frac{1.31951-1.31951^{11}}{1-1.31951}=6195\)代数/微积分
3货币时间价值L01
Eric deposits 100 into a savings account at time 0, which pays interest at an annual nominal rate of \(i\), compounded semiannually. Mike deposits 200 into a different savings account at time 0, which pays simple interest at an annual rate of \(i\). Eric and Mike earn the same amount of interest during the last 6 months of the 8th year. Calculate \(i\).
(A) 9.06%(B) 9.26%(C) 9.46%(D) 9.66%(E) 9.86%
复利对单利利息
答案 C
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 写复利后半年利息\(100\big(1+\tfrac{i}{2}\big)^{15}\tfrac{i}{2}\)L01
② 等于同期单利利息\(100\big(1+\tfrac{i}{2}\big)^{15}\tfrac{i}{2}=200\tfrac{i}{2}\)L01
③ 解半年因子求i\(\big(1+\tfrac{i}{2}\big)^{15}=2\Rightarrow i=9.46\%\)代数/微积分
4年金L04
A perpetuity costs 77.1 and makes end-of-year payments. The perpetuity pays 1 at the end of year 2, 2 at the end of year 3, ...., \(n\) at the end of year \((n+1)\). After year \((n+1)\), the payments remain constant at \(n\). The annual effective interest rate is 10.5%. Calculate \(n\).
(A) 17(B) 18(C) 19(D) 20(E) 21
递增后持平永续
答案 C
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 现值拆递增加永续尾\(77.1=v(Ia)_{\overline{n}|}+\frac{nv^{n+1}}{i}\)L04
② 化简成年金除以i\(77.1=\frac{a_{\overline{n}|}}{i}=\frac{1-v^n}{0.011025}\)L04
③ 解贴现幂求n\(1.105^{-n}=0.14997\Rightarrow n=19\)代数/微积分
5年金L05
1000 is deposited into Fund X, which earns an annual effective rate of 6%. At the end of each year, the interest earned plus an additional 100 is withdrawn from the fund. At the end of the tenth year, the fund is depleted. The annual withdrawals of interest and principal are deposited into Fund Y, which earns an annual effective rate of 9%. Calculate the accumulated value of Fund Y at the end of year 10.
(A) 1519(B) 1819(C) 2085(D) 2273(E) 2431
取款再投资累积
答案 C
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 利息成递减年金\(6(Ds)_{\overline{10}|0.09}+100s_{\overline{10}|0.09}\)L05
② 展开递减年金终值\(6\Big(\frac{10(1.09)^{10}-s_{\overline{10}|0.09}}{0.09}\Big)=565.38\)L04
③ 两项相加收口\(565.38+1519.29=2084.67\)代数/微积分
6贷款L06
A 20-year loan of 1000 is repaid with payments at the end of each year. Each of the first ten payments equals 150% of the amount of interest due. Each of the last ten payments is \(X\). The lender charges interest at an annual effective rate of 10%. Calculate \(X\).
(A) 32(B) 57(C) 70(D) 97(E) 117
付息150%还款
答案 D
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 多付5%逐年削本金\(1000(1-0.05)^{10}=598.74\)L06
② 后10年等额清偿\(598.74=Xa_{\overline{10}|10\%}=6.1446X\)L03
③ 解年还款额\(X=97.44\)代数/微积分
7债券L07
A 10,000 par value 10-year bond with 8% annual coupons is bought at a premium to yield an annual effective rate of 6%. Calculate the interest portion of the 7th coupon.
(A) 632(B) 642(C) 651(D) 660(E) 667
溢价债息票利息份额
答案 B
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 账面值=未来款现值\(BV_6=10000v^4+800a_{\overline{4}|0.06}=10693\)L07
② 利息份额=账面值乘i\(10693\times 0.06=641.58\)L07
8年金L04
A perpetuity-immediate pays 100 per year. Immediately after the fifth payment, the perpetuity is exchanged for a 25-year annuity-immediate that will pay \(X\) at the end of the first year. Each subsequent annual payment will be 8% greater than the preceding payment. The annual effective rate of interest is 8%. Calculate \(X\).
(A) 54(B) 64(C) 74(D) 84(E) 94
永续换等比年金
答案 A
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 第5付后永续价值\(100/0.08=1250\)L03
② 等比年金现值恒定\(1250=X(v+1.08v^2+\cdots+1.08^{24}v^{25})=X\cdot 25/1.08\)L04
③ 解首期付款\(X=50(1.08)=54\)代数/微积分
9货币时间价值L01
Jeff deposits 10 into a fund today and 20 fifteen years later. Interest for the first 10 years is credited at a nominal discount rate of \(d\) compounded quarterly, and thereafter at a nominal interest rate of 6% compounded semiannually. The accumulated balance in the fund at the end of 30 years is 100. Calculate \(d\).
(A) 4.33%(B) 4.43%(C) 4.53%(D) 4.63%(E) 4.73%
名义贴现率分段
答案 C
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 30年末价值方程\(10(1-d/4)^{-40}(1.03)^{40}+20(1.03)^{30}=100\)L02
② 分离贴现因子\(10(1-d/4)^{-40}=\frac{100-20(1.03)^{30}}{1.03^{40}}=15.7738\)代数/微积分
③ 解名义贴现率\(1-\tfrac{d}{4}=1.57738^{-1/40}=0.98867\Rightarrow d=4(1-0.98867)=4.53\%\)L01
10货币时间价值L01
Ernie makes deposits of 100 at time 0, and \(X\) at time 3. The fund grows at a force of interest \(\delta_t = \frac{t^2}{100}\), \(t > 0\). The amount of interest earned from time 3 to time 6 is also \(X\). Calculate \(X\).
(A) 385(B) 485(C) 585(D) 685(E) 785
变力度求利息
答案 E
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 积分力度得累积函数\(a(t)=\exp\big(\int_0^t \tfrac{s^2}{100}ds\big)=\exp(t^3/300)\)L01
② 100累积到时3\(100\exp(27/300)=109.41743\)L01
③ 时3到6利息等于X\((109.41743+X)[a(6)/a(3)-1]=X\)L02
④ 解出X\(96.026159=0.122387X\Rightarrow X=784.61\)代数/微积分
11年金L04
Mike buys a perpetuity-immediate with varying annual payments. During the first 5 years, the payment is constant and equal to 10. Beginning in year 6, the payments start to increase. For year 6 and all future years, the payment in that year is \(K\)% larger than the payment in the year immediately preceding that year, where \(K < 9.2\). At an annual effective interest rate of 9.2%, the perpetuity has a present value of 167.50. Calculate \(K\).
(A) 4.0(B) 4.2(C) 4.4(D) 4.6(E) 4.8
等比增长永续求K
答案 A
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 前5年年金加等比尾\(167.50=10a_{\overline{5}|9.2\%}+10(1.092)^{-5}\sum_{t=1}^{\infty}\big[\tfrac{1+k}{1.092}\big]^t\)L04
② 几何级数求和\(128.8045=135.2445\,\tfrac{1+k}{1.092}\)代数/微积分
③ 解增长率\(1+k=1.04\Rightarrow K=4.0\%\)代数/微积分
12贷款L06
A 10-year loan of 2000 is to be repaid with payments at the end of each year. It can be repaid under the following two options: (i) Equal annual payments at an annual effective interest rate of 8.07%. (ii) Installments of 200 each year plus interest on the unpaid balance at an annual effective interest rate of \(i\). The sum of the payments under option (i) equals the sum of the payments under option (ii). Calculate \(i\).
(A) 8.75%(B) 9.00%(C) 9.25%(D) 9.50%(E) 9.75%
两种还款方式比较
答案 B
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 方式一求等额还款\(2000=Pa_{\overline{10}|0.0807}\Rightarrow P=299\)L06
② 总还2990利息990\(990=i[2000+1800+\cdots+200]\)L06
③ 解利率\(990=11000i\Rightarrow i=9.00\%\)代数/微积分
13贷款L06 · L04
A loan is amortized over five years with monthly payments at an annual nominal interest rate of 9% compounded monthly. The first payment is 1000 and is to be paid one month from the date of the loan. Each succeeding monthly payment will be 2% lower than the prior payment. Calculate the outstanding loan balance immediately after the 40th payment is made.
(A) 6750(B) 6890(C) 6940(D) 7030(E) 7340
等比还款余额
答案 B
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 余额前瞻取后20期\(OB_{40}=1000[0.98^{40}v+\cdots+0.98^{59}v^{20}]\)L06
② 几何级数求和\(OB_{40}=1000\frac{0.98^{40}v-0.98^{60}v^{21}}{1-0.98v},\;v=\tfrac{1}{1.0075}\)L04
③ 数值收口\(1000\frac{0.44238-0.25434}{1-0.97270}=6888\)代数/微积分
14年金L03
To accumulate 8000 at the end of \(3n\) years, deposits of 98 are made at the end of each of the first \(n\) years and 196 at the end of each of the next \(2n\) years. The annual effective rate of interest is \(i\). You are given \((1+i)^n = 2.0\). Calculate \(i\).
(A) 11.25%(B) 11.75%(C) 12.25%(D) 12.75%(E) 13.25%
分段存款累积
答案 C
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 双段年金终值方程\(98s_{\overline{3n}|}+98s_{\overline{2n}|}=8000\)L02
② 代入翻倍条件\((1+i)^n=2\Rightarrow \tfrac{8-1}{i}+\tfrac{4-1}{i}=81.63\)L03
③ 解利率\(\tfrac{10}{i}=81.63\Rightarrow i=12.25\%\)代数/微积分
15年金L04
Olga buys a 5-year increasing annuity for \(X\). Olga will receive 2 at the end of the first month, 4 at the end of the second month, and for each month thereafter the payment increases by 2. The annual nominal interest rate is 9% convertible quarterly. Calculate \(X\).
(A) 2680(B) 2730(C) 2780(D) 2830(E) 2880
月递增年金现值
答案 B
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 季名义换月实利率\((1+j)^3=1+\tfrac{0.09}{4}\Rightarrow j=0.00744\)L01
② 套递增年金公式\(2(Ia)_{\overline{60}|0.00744}=2\frac{\ddot{a}_{\overline{60}|}-60v^{60}}{0.00744}\)L04
③ 数值收口\(2\frac{48.6136-38.4592}{0.00744}=2729.7\)代数/微积分
16货币时间价值L02
David can receive one of the following two payment streams: (i) 100 at time 0, 200 at time \(n\) years, and 300 at time \(2n\) years (ii) 600 at time 10 years At an annual effective interest rate of \(i\), the present values of the two streams are equal. Given \(v^n = 0.76\), calculate \(i\).
(A) 3.5%(B) 4.0%(C) 4.5%(D) 5.0%(E) 5.5%
两流现值相等
答案 A
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 两流现值相等\(100+200v^n+300v^{2n}=600v^{10}\)L02
② 代入已知贴现幂\(100+200(0.76)+300(0.76)^2=425.28=600v^{10}\)代数/微积分
③ 解利率\(v=0.96617\Rightarrow i=3.5\%\)代数/微积分
17货币时间价值L01
Payments are made to an account at a continuous rate of \((8k + tk)\), where \(0 \le t \le 10\). Interest is credited at a force of interest \(\delta_t = \frac{1}{8+t}\). After time 10, the account is worth 20,000. Calculate \(k\).
(A) 111(B) 116(C) 121(D) 126(E) 131
连续缴存变力度
答案 A
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 积分力度得累积函数\(a(t)=e^{\int_0^t\frac{dr}{8+r}}=\frac{8+t}{8}\)L01
② 连续缴存终值方程\(20000=\int_0^{10}(8k+tk)\tfrac{a(10)}{a(t)}dt=k\int_0^{10}18\,dt\)L02
③ 解出k\(k=\tfrac{20000}{180}=111\)代数/微积分
18债券L07
You have decided to invest in Bond X, an \(n\)-year bond with semi-annual coupons and the following characteristics: (i) Par value is 1000. (ii) The ratio of the semi-annual coupon rate, \(r\), to the desired semi-annual yield rate, \(i\), is 1.03125. (iii) The present value of the redemption value is 381.50. Given \((1+i)^{-n} = 0.5889\), calculate the price of bond X.
(A) 1019(B) 1029(C) 1050(D) 1055(E) 1072
息票收益率比求价
答案 D
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 债券价格基本式\(X=1000r\,a_{\overline{2n}|}+Cv^{2n}\)L07
② 代入息率收益率比\(X=1000(1.03125)(1-0.5889^2)+381.50\)代数/微积分
③ 数值收口\(X=1055.11\)代数/微积分
19货币时间价值L05
Project P requires an investment of 4000 today. The investment pays 2000 one year from today and 4000 two years from today. Project Q requires an investment of \(X\) two years from today. The investment pays 2000 today and 4000 one year from today. The net present values of the two projects are equal at an annual effective interest rate of 10%. Calculate \(X\).
(A) 5400(B) 5420(C) 5440(D) 5460(E) 5480
两项目NPV相等
答案 D
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 两项目NPV相等\(-4000+2000v+4000v^2=2000+4000v-Xv^2\)L05
② 代入v=1/1.1化简\(\frac{4000+X}{1.21}=6000+\frac{2000}{1.1}\)代数/微积分
③ 解X\(X=5460\)代数/微积分
20年金L03
A perpetuity-immediate pays \(X\) per year. Brian receives the first \(n\) payments, Colleen receives the next \(n\) payments, and a charity receives the remaining payments. Brian's share of the present value of the original perpetuity is 40%, and the charity's share is \(K\). Calculate \(K\).
(A) 24%(B) 28%(C) 32%(D) 36%(E) 40%
永续分段份额
答案 D
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 前n年占永续4成\(Xa_{\overline{n}|}=0.4\tfrac{X}{i}\Rightarrow v^n=0.6\)L03
② 慈善得2n后尾巴\(K=v^{2n}\tfrac{X}{i}=0.36\tfrac{X}{i}\)L03
③ 份额收口\(K=36\%\)代数/微积分
21贷款L06
Seth, Janice, and Lori each borrow 5000 for five years at an annual nominal interest rate of 12%, compounded semi-annually. Seth has interest accumulated over the five years and pays all the interest and principal in a lump sum at the end of five years. Janice pays interest at the end of every six-month period as it accrues and the principal at the end of five years. Lori repays her loan with 10 level payments at the end of every six-month period. Calculate the total amount of interest paid on all three loans.
(A) 8718(B) 8728(C) 8738(D) 8748(E) 8758
三种还法总利息
答案 D
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① Seth趸还复利利息\(5000\big[(1+\tfrac{0.12}{2})^{10}-1\big]=3954.24\)L01
② Janice每年付息\(5000(0.06)(10)=3000\)L06
③ Lori等额摊还利息\(P=\tfrac{5000}{a_{\overline{10}|6\%}}=679.35,\;10P-5000=1793.40\)L06
④ 三人合计\(3954.24+3000+1793.40=8747.64\)代数/微积分
22货币时间价值L01
Bruce and Robbie each open up new bank accounts at time 0. Bruce deposits 100 into his bank account, and Robbie deposits 50 into his. Each account earns the same annual effective interest rate. The amount of interest earned in Bruce's account during the 11th year is equal to \(X\). The amount of interest earned in Robbie's account during the 17th year is also equal to \(X\). Calculate \(X\).
(A) 28.00(B) 31.30(C) 34.60(D) 36.70(E) 38.90
两账户年利息等
答案 E
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① Bruce第11年利息\(X=100[(1+i)^{11}-(1+i)^{10}]=100(1+i)^{10}i\)L01
② Robbie第17年利息\(X=50(1+i)^{16}i\)L01
③ 两式相除解i\(1=0.5(1+i)^6\Rightarrow i=2^{1/6}-1=0.122462\)代数/微积分
④ 回代求X\(X=100(1.122462)^{10}(0.122462)=38.879\)代数/微积分
23贷款L06
Ron is repaying a loan with payments of 1 at the end of each year for \(n\) years. The annual effective interest rate on the loan is \(i\). The amount of interest paid in year \(t\) plus the amount of principal repaid in year \(t + 1\) equals \(X\). Determine which of the following is equal to \(X\).
(A) \(1 + \frac{v^{n-t}}{i}\)(B) \(1 + \frac{v^{n-t}}{d}\)(C) \(1 + v^{n-t} i\)(D) \(1 + v^{n-t} d\)(E) \(1 + v^{n-t}\)
利息加本金恒等式
答案 D
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 第t年利息份额\(ia_{\overline{n-t+1}|}=1-v^{n-t+1}\)L06
② 第t+1年本金份额\(1-(1-v^{n-t})=v^{n-t}\)L06
③ 相加化简\(X=1-v^{n-t+1}+v^{n-t}=1+v^{n-t}d\)代数/微积分
24年金L03
At an annual effective interest rate of \(i\), \(i > 0\%\), the present value of a perpetuity paying 10 at the end of each 3-year period, with the first payment at the end of year 3, is 32. At the same annual effective rate of \(i\), the present value of a perpetuity paying 1 at the end of each 4-month period, with first payment at the end of 4 months, is \(X\). Calculate \(X\).
(A) 31.6(B) 32.6(C) 33.6(D) 34.6(E) 35.6
异频永续换算
答案 B
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 三年一付永续现值\(32=\tfrac{10v^3}{1-v^3}\)L03
② 解贴现因子\(v^3=\tfrac{32}{42}\)代数/微积分
③ 四月一付套同式\(X=\frac{(32/42)^{1/9}}{1-(32/42)^{1/9}}=32.599\)L03
25久期凸性免疫L08
As of 12/31/2013, an insurance company has a known obligation to pay 1,000,000 on 12/31/2017. To fund this liability, the company immediately purchases 4-year 5% annual coupon bonds totaling 822,703 of par value. The company anticipates reinvestment interest rates to remain constant at 5% through 12/31/2017. The maturity value of the bond equals the par value. Consider two reinvestment interest rate movement scenarios effective 1/1/2014. Scenario A has interest rates drop by 0.5%. Scenario B has interest rates increase by 0.5%. Determine which of the following best describes the insurance company's profit or (loss) as of 12/31/2017 after the liability is paid.
(A) Scenario A - 6,610, Scenario B - 11,150(B) Scenario A - (14,760), Scenario B - 14,420(C) Scenario A - (18,910), Scenario B - 19,190(D) Scenario A - (1,310), Scenario B - 1,320(E) Scenario A - 0, Scenario B - 0
再投资利率风险
答案 D
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 每年息票再投额\(822703\times 0.05=41135\)L08
② 情景A按4.5%再投\(41135\,s_{\overline{4}|0.045}=41135(4.2782)=175984\)L03
③ 加到期值算损益\(175984+822703-1000000=-1313\)代数/微积分
26年金L04
An insurance company has an obligation to pay the medical costs for a claimant. Annual claim costs today are 5000, and medical inflation is expected to be 7% per year. The claimant will receive 20 payments. Claim payments are made at yearly intervals, with the first claim payment to be made one year from today. Calculate the present value of the obligation using an annual effective interest rate of 5%.
(A) 87,900(B) 102,500(C) 114,600(D) 122,600(E) Cannot be determined
医疗通胀等比现值
答案 D
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 等比现金流现值\(5000[1.07v+1.07^2v^2+\cdots+1.07^{20}v^{20}]\)L04
② 几何级数求和收口\(5000\frac{1.01905-1.48622}{1-1.01905}=122617\)代数/微积分
27货币时间价值L05

① 平价债久期=期初年金\(d_0 = \ddot{a}_{\overline{8}|0.05} = 6.7864\)L08
② 付息前久期少一年\(d_1 = d_0 - 1 = 5.7864\)L08
③ 付息后按7年债\(d_2 = \ddot{a}_{\overline{7}|0.05} = 6.0757\)L08
④ 比值收口\(\dfrac{d_1}{d_2} = \dfrac{5.7864}{6.0757} = 0.9524\)代数/微积分
54久期凸性免疫L08
An insurance company must pay liabilities of 99 at the end of one year, 102 at the end of two years and 100 at the end of three years. The only investments available to the company are the following three bonds. Bond A and Bond C are annual coupon bonds. Bond B is a zero-coupon bond. Bond, Maturity (in years), Yield-to-Maturity (Annualized), Coupon Rate | A, 1, 6%, 7% | B, 2, 7%, 0% | C, 3, 9%, 5% All three bonds have a par value of 100 and will be redeemed at par. Calculate the number of units of Bond A that must be purchased to match the liabilities exactly.
(A) 0.8807(B) 0.8901(C) 0.8975(D) 0.9524(E) 0.9724
三债精确匹配
答案 A
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 末期负债配C债\(N_C(105) = 100 \Rightarrow N_C = 0.9524\)L08
② 扣C息票回推B债\(N_B(100) = 102 - 0.9524(5) \Rightarrow N_B = 0.9724\)L08
③ 扣息票回推A债\(N_A(107) = 99 - 0.9524(5) \Rightarrow N_A = 0.8807\)L08
55久期凸性免疫L08
Determine which of the following statements is false with respect to Redington immunization.
(A) Modified duration may change at different rates for each of the assets and liabilities as time goes by.(B) Redington immunization requires infrequent rebalancing to keep modified duration of assets equal to modified duration of liabilities.(C) This technique is designed to work only for small changes in the interest rate.(D) The yield curve is assumed to be flat.(E) The yield curve shifts in parallel when the interest rate changes.
Redington辨析
答案 B
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 列免疫条件逐项判\(P_A = P_L,\ P'_A = P'_L,\ P''_A > P''_L\)L08
② B错:免疫需频繁再平衡\(\text{B 为唯一假命题}\)L08

63货币时间价值L01
Bill and Joe each put 10 into separate accounts at time \(t = 0\), where \(t\) is measured in years. Bill's account earns interest at a constant annual effective interest rate of \(K/25\), \(K > 0\). Joe's account earns interest at a force of interest, \(\delta_t = \frac{1}{K + 0.25t}\). At the end of four years, the amount in each account is \(X\). Calculate \(X\).
(A) 20.7(B) 21.7(C) 22.7(D) 23.7(E) 24.7
实际利率对力度
答案 A
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 两种累积相等方程\(10\left(1+\dfrac{K}{25}\right)^4 = 10\exp\left(\int_0^4 \dfrac{dt}{K+0.25t}\right)\)L01
② 积分算力度累积\(\int_0^4 \dfrac{dt}{K+0.25t} = 4\ln\dfrac{K+1}{K}\)L01
③ 化简解K\(1+0.04K = \dfrac{K+1}{K} \Rightarrow 0.04K^2 = 1 \Rightarrow K = 5\)代数/微积分
④ 求X收口\(X = 10(1+5/25)^4 = 20.74\)代数/微积分

③ 贷款额=还款现值\(L = 2500a_{\overline{25}|} + v^{25}\,100(Da)_{\overline{25}|}\)L06
④ 首期利息化简收口\(I_1 = iL = 2500 - Xv^{25}\)L06

② 隔年存分段积累\(100\ddot{s}_{\overline{5}|0.0816}(1.05)^4 + 100\ddot{s}_{\overline{2}|0.1025} = 659.269\)L03
③ 两年收益率方程\(100\ddot{s}_{\overline{5}|j} = 659.269 \Rightarrow j = 0.093637\)L05
④ 年化收口\(1.093637^{0.5} - 1 = 4.58\%\)代数/微积分

100久期凸性免疫L08
Annuity A pays 1 at the beginning of each year for three years. Annuity B pays 1 at the beginning of each year for four years. The Macaulay duration of Annuity A at the time of purchase is 0.93. 102久期凸性免疫L08
Rhonda purchases a perpetuity providing a payment of 1 at the beginning of each year. The perpetuity's Macaulay duration is 30 years. Calculate the modified duration of this perpetuity.

103久期凸性免疫L08
Which of the following statements regarding immunization are true? I. If long-term interest rates are lower than short-term rates, the need for immunization is reduced. II. Either Macaulay or modified duration can be used to develop an immunization strategy. III. Both processes of matching the present values of the flows or the flows themselves will produce exact matching.
(A) I only(B) II only(C) III only(D) I, II and III(E) The correct answer is not given by (A), (B), (C), or (D).
免疫命题辨析
答案 B
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 逐项判真伪\( \text{I 假, II 真, III 假} \)L08
② III错因:仅现值匹配不足\( PV_A=PV_L\ \text{在利率变动时不保证免疫} \)L08
104久期凸性免疫L08
A company owes 500 and 1000 to be paid at the end of year one and year four, respectively. The company will set up an investment program to match the duration and the present value of the above obligation using an annual effective interest rate of 10%. The investment program produces asset cash flows of \(X\) today and \(Y\) in three years. Calculate \(X\) and determine whether the investment program satisfies the conditions for Redington immunization.
(A) \(X = 75\) and the Redington immunization conditions are not satisfied.(B) \(X = 75\) and the Redington immunization conditions are satisfied.(C) \(X = 1138\) and the Redington immunization conditions are not satisfied.(D) \(X = 1138\) and the Redington immunization conditions are satisfied.(E) \(X = 1414\) and the Redington immunization conditions are satisfied.
Redington条件判定
答案 A
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 列现值函数及导数\( P(i)=X+Y(1+i)^{-3}-500(1+i)^{-1}-1000(1+i)^{-4} \)L08
② 现值久期双匹配方程\( P(0.1)=X+0.7513Y-1137.56=0,\ P'(0.1)=-2.0490Y+2896.91=0 \)L08
③ 解X与Y\( Y=\frac{2896.91}{2.0490}=1413.82,\ X=1137.56-0.7513(1413.82)=75.36 \)代数/微积分
④ 验二阶导判Redington\( P''(0.1)=-1506.34<0\ \Rightarrow \text{条件不满足} \)L08
105久期凸性免疫L08
An insurance company has a known liability of 1,000,000 that is due 8 years from now. The technique of full immunization is to be employed. Asset I will provide a cash flow of 300,000 exactly 6 years from now. Asset II will provide a cash flow of \(X\), exactly \(y\) years from now, where \(y > 8\). The annual effective interest rate is 4%. Calculate \(X\).
(A) 697,100(B) 698,600(C) 700,000(D) 701,500(E) 702,900
完全免疫求X
答案 D
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 以时点8列免疫方程\( P(i)=300000(1+i)^2+X(1+i)^{8-y}-1000000=0 \)L08
② 代4%求资产现值项\( X(1.04)^{-y}=\frac{1000000-300000(1.04)^2}{1.04^8}=493595.85 \)代数/微积分
③ 导数条件解时点y\( y=8+\frac{624000}{493595.85(1.04)^7}=8.9607 \)L08
④ 回代收口\( X=493595.85(1.04)^{8.9607}=701459 \)代数/微积分
106久期凸性免疫L08
A company has liabilities of 573 due at the end of year 2 and 701 due at the end of year 5. A portfolio comprises two zero-coupon bonds, Bond A and Bond B. Determine which portfolio produces a Redington immunization of the liabilities using an annual effective interest rate of 7.0%.
(A) Bond A: 1-year, current price 500; Bond B: 6-years, current price 500(B) Bond A: 1-year, current price 572; Bond B: 6-years, current price 428(C) Bond A: 3-years, current price 182; Bond B: 4-years, current price 1092(D) Bond A: 3-years, current price 637; Bond B: 4-years, current price 637(E) Bond A: 3.5 years, current price 1000; Bond B: Not used
Redington组合选择
答案 A
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 负债现值筛选组合\( \frac{573}{1.07^2}+\frac{701}{1.07^5}=1000\ \Rightarrow\ \text{仅A/B/E现值匹配} \)L08
② 久期匹配淘汰B\( D_L=\frac{2(573)/1.07^2+5(701)/1.07^5}{1000}=3.5,\ D_B=3.14 \)L08
③ 凸性比较定A\( C_L=14.5,\ C_A=\frac{500(1)+500(36)}{1000}=18.5>14.5,\ C_E=12.25 \)L08
107久期凸性免疫L08

答案 E

(A) \( \sum_{n=1}^{6} \frac{800}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{4}\right)^{2n-1}} = \sum_{n=1}^{36} \frac{X}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{4}\right)^{\frac{n-0.5}{3}}} \)(B) \( \sum_{n=1}^{6} \frac{800}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{12}\right)^{6n-3}} = \sum_{n=1}^{36} \frac{X}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{12}\right)^{n-0.5}} \)(C) \( 4000 + \sum_{n=1}^{6} \frac{800}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{4}\right)^{\frac{6n-2}{3}}} = \frac{4000}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{4}\right)^{12}} + \sum_{n=1}^{36} \frac{X}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{4}\right)^{\frac{n}{3}}} \)(D) \( 4000 + \sum_{n=1}^{6} \frac{800}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{12}\right)^{6n-3}} = \frac{4000}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{12}\right)^{36}} + \sum_{n=1}^{36} \frac{X}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{12}\right)^{n-0.5}} \)(E) \( 4000 + \sum_{n=1}^{6} \frac{800}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{4}\right)^{2n-1}} = \frac{4000}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{4}\right)^{12}} + \sum_{n=1}^{36} \frac{X}{\left(1+\frac{0.2640}{4}\right)^{\frac{n-0.5}{3}}} \)

The annual effective interest rate charged by the lender is 8% in the first year and \( i \) in the second year. The annual effective yield rate for the lender is 10%. Calculate \( i \).
(A) 12.8%(B) 12.9%(C) 13.0%(D) 13.1%(E) 13.2%
变利率贷款求i
答案 E
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 名义收益率求还款X\(100=\frac{X}{1.1}+\frac{2X}{1.1^2}\Rightarrow X=39.03\)L06
② 一年后未偿余额\(100+8-39.03=68.97\)L06
③ 第二年清偿解i\(68.97(1+i)=2(39.03)\Rightarrow i=\frac{78.06}{68.97}-1=13.2\%\)代数/微积分

181久期凸性免疫L08
Determine which of the following conditions are necessary for an immunization strategy. I. The present value of the cash inflow from the assets is equal to the present value of the cash outflow from the liabilities. II. The price sensitivity to changes in interest rates is greater for assets than for liabilities. III. The convexity of assets is less than the convexity of liabilities.
(A) I only(B) II only(C) III only(D) I, II, and III(E) The correct answer is not given by (A), (B), (C), or (D).
免疫必要条件
答案 A

① t=17时几何永续价值\(2500\frac{1+k}{0.035-k}\)L04

③ 线性化解增长率\(k = \frac{1.61 - 0.37631 - 0.55720}{46 - 10.7516 + 0.55720} = 0.01889 = 1.89\%\)代数/微积分

229久期凸性免疫L08

① 年付款按分段利率再投\(AV_{10} = \frac{L}{a_{\overline{10}|10\%}}\left(s_{\overline{4}|10\%}1.07^6 + s_{\overline{6}|7\%}\right)\)L05
② 总收益率消去本金L\(i = \left(\frac{4.6410(1.5007) + 7.1533}{6.1446}\right)^{1/10} - 1\)L05
③ 数值收口\(i = 8.67\%\)代数/微积分
231贷款L06
Two borrowers obtain loans at the same time. Each loan is for the same amount and is repaid with level end-of month payments. The first borrower is charged a monthly effective interest rate of \(i\) and makes payments of \(P\) for \(k\) months to pay off the loan, where \(k\) is a positive integer. You are given that \(0 < j < 0.04\) and that \(i = (1+j)^{5} - 1\). Determine which statement about \(P\) is true.

两贷款付款区间
答案 E
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 两贷款价值方程等本金\(P\cdot a_{\overline{k}|i} = 120\cdot a_{\overline{5k}|j},\ 1+i = (1+j)^5\)L06
② 年金比化简\(P = 120\frac{i}{j} = 120\frac{(1+j)^5 - 1}{j}\)L03
③ 0<j<0.04界定区间\(5 < \frac{(1+j)^5-1}{j} < 5.41633 \Rightarrow 600 < P < 650\)代数/微积分

Which of the following expressions represents a correct equation of value? 265货币时间价值L01
Consider two loans. Loan A has an initial principal of \(P_0\) and an annual nominal interest rate of \(i\), convertible monthly. Loan B also has an annual nominal interest rate of \(i\), but the interest is convertible daily. At the end of the first month, a payment of \(m\) is made on Loan A, which includes one month of interest. The remaining balance on Loan A is then \(P_1\). Let \(j\) be the monthly effective interest rate of Loan B, assuming there are 12 equal months in a year and 365 days in a year. Determine which of the following represents \(j\).
(A) \(\left[1 + \frac{1}{12}\left(\frac{P_1 - P_0 + m}{P_0}\right)\right]^{12} - 1\)(B) \(\left[1 + 12\left(\frac{P_1 - P_0 + m}{P_0}\right)\right]^{1/12} - 1\)(C) \(\left[1 + \frac{12}{365}\left(\frac{P_1 - P_0 + m}{P_0}\right)\right]^{12} - 1\)(D) \(\left[1 + \frac{365}{12}\left(\frac{P_1 - P_0 + m}{P_0}\right)\right]^{12/365} - 1\)(E) \(\left[1 + \frac{12}{365}\left(\frac{P_1 - P_0 + m}{P_0}\right)\right]^{365/12} - 1\)
月计对日计换算
答案 E
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 首月实际月利率\(\dfrac{P_1-(P_0-m)}{P_0}=\dfrac{P_1-P_0+m}{P_0}\)L01
② 乘12得名义年率\(12\left(\dfrac{P_1-P_0+m}{P_0}\right)\)L01
③ 日计率复利回月率\(\left[1+\dfrac{12}{365}\left(\dfrac{P_1-P_0+m}{P_0}\right)\right]^{365/12}-1\)L01

① 第11期后剩余年金PV\(10a_{\overline{9}|0.06}=68.0169\)L03
② 年率换半年实际率\(j=1.06^{1/2}-1=0.02956301\)L01

311货币时间价值L02
A credit card company charges an annual effective interest rate of 16.8%. Interest accumulates from the date of purchase. A borrower's credit card balance was X at the beginning of month 1. Starting with month 1, the borrower purchased satellite internet service, resulting in a 79.99 charge on the credit card at the middle of each month. The borrower paid 250 at the end of each month. Immediately after the payment in month 15, the balance was 3000. Determine which of the following is an equation of value that can be used to solve for X.
(A) \( X + \sum_{n=1}^{15} \frac{79.99}{(1.014)^{n-0.5}} = \frac{3000}{(1.014)^{15}} + \sum_{n=1}^{15} \frac{250}{(1.014)^{n}} \)(B) \( X + \sum_{n=1}^{16} \frac{79.99}{(1.168)^{\frac{n+0.5}{12}}} = \frac{3000}{(1.168)^{\frac{5}{4}}} + \sum_{n=1}^{16} \frac{250}{(1.168)^{\frac{n}{12}}} \)(C) \( X + \sum_{n=1}^{16} \frac{79.99}{(1.168)^{\frac{n-0.5}{12}}} = \frac{3000}{(1.168)^{\frac{4}{3}}} + \sum_{n=1}^{16} \frac{250}{(1.168)^{\frac{n}{12}}} \)(D) \( X + \sum_{n=1}^{15} \frac{79.99}{(1.168)^{\frac{n+0.5}{12}}} = \frac{3000}{(1.168)^{\frac{5}{4}}} + \sum_{n=1}^{15} \frac{250}{(1.168)^{\frac{n}{12}}} \)(E) \( X + \sum_{n=1}^{15} \frac{79.99}{(1.168)^{\frac{n-0.5}{12}}} = \frac{3000}{(1.168)^{\frac{5}{4}}} + \sum_{n=1}^{15} \frac{250}{(1.168)^{\frac{n}{12}}} \)
信用卡价值方程
答案 E
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 补记X与末付3000使净额零\(X+\sum_{n=1}^{15}\tfrac{79.99}{1.168^{(n-0.5)/12}}-\sum_{n=1}^{15}\tfrac{250}{1.168^{n/12}}-\tfrac{3000}{1.168^{5/4}}=0\)L02
② 移项得选项等式\(X+\sum_{n=1}^{15}\tfrac{79.99}{1.168^{(n-0.5)/12}}=\tfrac{3000}{1.168^{5/4}}+\sum_{n=1}^{15}\tfrac{250}{1.168^{n/12}}\)L02

① 每期还1共付n\(\text{总还款}=n\)L06
② 初始贷款额\(L=a_{\overline{n}|i}\)L06
③ 总利息为差额\(n-a_{\overline{n}|i}\)L06

382久期凸性免疫L08

390久期凸性免疫L08
Company ABC is considering the following three investments: i) Investment X is a 50-year zero-coupon bond ii) Investment Y is a perpetuity with annual payments iii) Investment Z is a geometrically increasing perpetuity with annual payments that increase at a rate of 3% per year For both perpetuities, the first payment will occur one year from now. The convexities of Investments X, Y, and Z are x, y, and z, respectively, based on an annual effective interest rate of 5%. Determine which expression represents the relationship between the convexity of the three investments.
(A) \( x < z < y \)(B) \( y < x < z \)(C) \( y < z < x \)(D) \( z < x < y \)(E) \( z < y < x \)
三投资凸性排序
答案 B

① 凸性定义P''/P\(C_x=P''(i)/P(i)\)L08
② 50年零息债凸性\(2550(1.05)^{-52}/1.05^{-50}=2550/1.05^2=2313\)L08
③ 永续与递增永续凸性\(2/0.05^2=800,\ 2/(0.05-0.03)^2=5000\)L08
④ 从低到高排序收口\(800<2313<5000\Rightarrow y<x<z\)代数/微积分
391货币时间价值L05
A company is considering a project where it expects to pay and receive the following cash flows: End of year, Cash flow | 2, Receives X | 4, Pays Y | 6, Receives X When calculated using an annual effective rate of i (i > 0), the present value of this project is equal to 0. Determine i.

At today's annual effective interest rate, the bonds have the following characteristics: Bond 1: Present Value 20,400, Modified Duration (in years) 11.735 | Bond 2: Present Value 20,400, Modified Duration (in years) 13.101 If the annual effective interest rate decreases by 50 basis points today, the first-order Macaulay approximations of the present value for Bond 1 and Bond 2 are 21,635.83 and \(X\), respectively. (A) 21,503.55(B) 21,596.97(C) 21,736.30(D) 21,779.69(E) 21,784.47
一阶Macaulay近似
答案 E
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 债1标定近似因子\(21{,}635.83=20{,}400\left(\frac{1+i_0}{1+i}\right)^{11.735(1+i)}\Rightarrow \left(\frac{1+i_0}{1+i}\right)^{11.735(1+i)}=1.060579902\)L08
② 换成债2久期幂\(1.060579902^{13.101/11.735}=1.067865963\)代数/微积分
③ 债2一阶Mac近似价\(P=20{,}400(1.067865963)=21{,}784.47\)L08

It provides payments of 100 today, 100 one month from now, 105 two months from now, 105 three months from now, and so on until the 83rd and 84th payments of 305 each are made. 447久期凸性免疫L08
A perpetuity-immediate with level annual payments of \(k\) has a Macaulay duration of 32.25 years based on an annual effective interest rate of \(i\). At the same annual effective interest rate, a perpetuity-due with level annual payments of \(1.02k\) has a modified duration of \(X\) years. Calculate \(X\).

永续due修正久期
答案 A
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 即期永续久期反解i\(D_{mac}=\frac{1+i}{i}=32.25\Rightarrow d=\frac{1}{32.25}\Rightarrow i=3.2\%\)L08
② due永续Mac久期\(D_{mac}=\frac{1}{i}=\frac{1}{0.032}=31.25\)L08
③ 折算修正久期\(D_{mod}=\frac{31.25}{1.032}=30.281\)L08

A twelve-year 2500 face amount bond has an annual coupon rate of 4.84% paid quarterly and is redeemable for \(C\). The book values of the bond following the 4th and 19th coupons are 2092.88 and 2316.30, respectively. Calculate the amount for accumulation of discount in the last coupon.

A 30-year 1000 face amount bond has an annual coupon rate of 7% paid semiannually for the first 15 years, and an annual coupon rate of 9% paid semiannually for the last 15 years. 450久期凸性免疫L08
An electric company faces liabilities with present values 24,000 and 1,000, due 7.5 years from now and 20 years from now, respectively. The company will purchase an \(n\)-year zero-coupon bond and a \(2n\)-year zero-coupon bond. Determine which of the following expressions describes the set of all values of \(n\) for which the company can achieve Redington immunization.
(A) \(4 \le n \le 8\)(B) \(5 < n < 7\)(C) \(n = 5\) or \(n = 7\)(D) \(0 < n < 5\) or \(n > 7\)(E) \(4 \le n < 5\) or \(7 < n \le 8\)
Redington可行n域
答案 B
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 现值久期匹配\(24{,}000+1{,}000=25{,}000,\ \frac{24{,}000(7.5)+1{,}000(20)}{25{,}000}=8\)L08
② 久期约束解占比f\(8=fn+(1-f)2n\Rightarrow f=2-8/n\)L08
③ 凸性不等式\((2-8/n)n^2+(8/n-1)4n^2>70\Rightarrow -2n^2+24n>70\)L08
④ 因式分解收口\(n^2-12n+35<0\Rightarrow (n-7)(n-5)<0\Rightarrow 5<n<7\)代数/微积分

Paul makes level deposits of 1000 into a fund at the beginning of each quarter for five years. The first deposit occurs at \(t = 0\), where \(t\) is in years. Starting at \(t = 5\), the amount of each quarterly deposit is 2% greater than the preceding deposit. The last such deposit occurs at \(t = 19.75\). ④ 合计收口\(48{,}138.59+161{,}639.07=209{,}778\)代数/微积分
452货币时间价值L05
An investment project involves an outlay of 30 at time 0 and 40 at time 1, where time is measured in years. In return the investor will receive 60 at time 2 and 90 at time \(n\), where \(n \ge 3\). Determine which one of the following statements about the annual effective yield rate is true.
(A) There is a unique yield rate, which is higher than 50%.(B) There is a unique yield rate, which is lower than 50%.(C) There are multiple yield rates, but all are higher than 50%.(D) There are multiple yield rates, but all are lower than 50%.(E) There are multiple yield rates with at least one lower than 50% and at least one higher than 50%.
收益率唯一性判定
答案 B
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 支出先于收入故唯一\(-30-40/1.5+60/1.5^2+90/1.5^n=0\)L05
② 50%利率下解n\(1.5^n=3\Rightarrow n=\ln 3/\ln 1.5=2.71<3\)代数/微积分
③ 末笔更晚判界\(n=3\ \text{时须}\ i<50\%\)L05

Kelly purchases a 25-year annual coupon bond for 20,000 with an annual effective yield rate of \(i\). The amount for the accumulation of discount in the first coupon is 50. ② 16期比值消元\(2.57114=\frac{(1+i)^{16}-1}{(1+i)^8-1}=(1+i)^8+1\)代数/微积分
③ 解收益率\((1+i)^8=1.57114\Rightarrow i=0.0581\)代数/微积分
④ 赎回值收口\(C=20{,}000+50s_{\overline{25}|i}=20{,}000+2671=22{,}671\)L07

455债券L07

③ X价与年收益率\(P_X=1073.78-138.88=934.90,\ i=1.015^4-1=0.06136\)L07

The modified durations of Investment A and Investment B are 4 years and \(Y\) years, respectively, each based on an annual effective interest rate of 10%. Calculate \(Y\).

459久期凸性免疫L08
A perpetuity pays 10,000 at the beginning of each year. The present value of the payments calculated using an annual effective interest rate of 7% is \(L\). The annual effective interest rate decreases to 5% immediately after the perpetuity is purchased. Using the first-order modified duration approximation, the estimated present value of the payments is \(M\). Calculate \(M - L\).
(A) 40,816(B) 43,673(C) 43,791(D) 47,290(E) 57,143
永续一阶修正估价
答案 A
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 永续due负债现值\(L=\frac{10{,}000}{0.07}(1.07)=152{,}857.14\)L08
② Mac久期比式\(\bar d=\frac{(Ia)_{\overline{\infty}|}}{\ddot a_{\overline{\infty}|}}=\frac{\frac{1}{0.07}+\frac{1}{0.07^2}}{\frac{1}{0.07}(1.07)}=14.2857\)L08
③ 折算修正久期\(\bar v=\frac{14.285714}{1.07}=13.351135\)L08
④ 一阶近似求差额\(M=152{,}857.14[1-(-0.02)(13.351135)]=193{,}673.47,\ M-L=40{,}816.33\)L08
460久期凸性免疫L08
A geometric perpetuity-immediate provides annual payments. The first payment is 1, and each subsequent payment is 0.5% less than the previous payment. Let \(M\) be the price of this perpetuity using an annual effective interest rate of 6.5%. The price should have been calculated using an annual effective interest rate of 5.5%. Let \(P\) be the correct price of this perpetuity and let \(E\) be the estimate of \(P\) based on the initial price, \(M\), using the first-order modified approximation. Calculate \(\frac{E-P}{P}\), the percentage error of the estimate.
(A) -2.78%(B) -2.04%(C) -1.92%(D) -1.24%(E) -1.06%
修正近似百分误差
答案 B
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 几何永续现值\(P(i)=\frac{1}{i-r}=\frac{1}{i+0.005}\)L08
② 求修正久期\(\bar v=-\frac{P'(i)}{P(i)}=\frac{1}{i+0.005}\)L08
③ 一阶修正近似式\(E=P(i_0)\left[1-(i-i_0)\bar v\right]=\frac{1}{i_0+0.005}\left(1-\frac{i-i_0}{i_0+0.005}\right)\)L08
④ 代0.065/0.055算误差\(\frac{E-P}{P}=-0.0204=-2.04\%\)代数/微积分
461久期凸性免疫L08
A geometric perpetuity-due provides annual payments. The first payment is 1, and each subsequent payment is 2% less than the previous payment. Let \(M\) be the price of this perpetuity using an annual effective interest rate of 8%. The price should have been calculated using an annual effective interest rate of 7%. Let \(P\) be the correct price of this perpetuity and let \(E\) be the estimate of \(P\) based on the initial price, \(M\), using the first-order Macaulay approximation. Calculate \(\frac{E-P}{P}\), the percentage error of the estimate.
(A) -1.48%(B) -1.16%(C) -0.92%(D) -0.49%(E) -0.26%
Mac近似百分误差
答案 D
步骤用的公式 / 定理出处
① 几何永续due现值\(P(i)=\frac{1+i}{i-r}=\frac{1+i}{i+0.02}\)L08
② 求Mac久期\(\bar d=(1+i)\bar v=\frac{0.98}{i+0.02}\)L08
③ 一阶Mac近似式\(E=P(i_0)\left(\frac{1+i_0}{1+i}\right)^{D_{mac}(i_0)}=\left(\frac{1+i_0}{i_0+0.02}\right)\left(\frac{1+i_0}{1+i}\right)^{\frac{1-0.02}{i_0+0.02}}\)L08
④ 代0.08/0.07算误差\(\frac{E-P}{P}=-0.004883=-0.49\%\)代数/微积分
